[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavif_fuzztest_yuvrgb@YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the libavif [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary during fuzz testing. The issue occurs in the `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction when performing a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte read operation, resulting in an out-of-bounds [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory access on the stack. The vulnerability was discovered through the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avif_fuzztest_yuvrgb@YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert` fuzzer and has been assigned a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscariness score of [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as an AddressSanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASan[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m error reporting a [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdynamic-stack-buffer-overflow during the execution of YUV to RGB color space [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconversion operations in the libavif library. The vulnerability is triggered when [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing image data through the conversion pipeline.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is classified as a **dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow** with a READ [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation of [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes at an invalid memory address. This represents a memory safety [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mviolation where the code attempts to read beyond the boundaries of a [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-allocated buffer.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Location of the Error**: The overflow occurs at [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/libavif/src/[0m[95mreformat.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m812:46[0m[39m` in the `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` function.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Stack**: The error originates from the following call chain:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere the actual overflow occurs[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `avifImageYUVToRGBImpl` [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `avifImageYUVToRGB`[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test harness function `Convert` in `avif_fuzztest_yuvrgb.cc`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Access Pattern**: The attempted read at address `[0m[1;36m0x7ffd4a345f9c[0m[39m` is in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma region marked as [0m[32m"Right alloca redzone [0m[32m([0m[32mcb[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m according to the ASan shadow memory [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdump. This indicates the code is attempting to read just beyond the end of a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-allocated buffer.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Test Parameters**: The fuzzer is testing the Convert function with multiple [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameters including:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - An avifImage unique pointer[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Integer values for dimensions and settings[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Enumeration values for `avifChromaUpsampling` and `avifChromaDownsampling`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Multiple boolean flags[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - An integer parameter[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Execution Environment**: The issue was reproduced using:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Docker container with ASAN enabled[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - libFuzzer with entropic power schedule[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;36m197[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m594[0m[39m inline [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-bit counters and PC tables loaded[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - RSS limit of [0m[1;36m2560[0m[39m MB and timeout of [0m[1;36m25[0m[39m seconds[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a comprehensive understanding of this issue, the following parts of the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase should be examined:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Location - `[0m[35m/src/libavif/src/[0m[95mreformat.c[0m[39m`**:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m in `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` where the overflow occurs[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function's buffer allocation and boundary calculations[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The logic determining read/write offsets during YUV to RGB conversion[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Calling Functions**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `avifImageYUVToRGBImpl` at line [0m[1;36m1713[0m[39m in reformat.c[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `avifImageYUVToRGB` at line [0m[1;36m1844[0m[39m in reformat.c[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The parameter validation and buffer sizing logic in these functions[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Image Structure**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `avifImage` structure definition and its memory layout[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How image dimensions, bit depths, and chroma subsampling parameters affect [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer allocations[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The relationship between input image properties and buffer size calculations[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Color Space Conversion Logic**:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The YUV to RGB conversion algorithms, particularly focusing on edge cases[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Chroma upsampling and downsampling implementations[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pixel format handling for different bit depths and color configurations[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Test Case Analysis**:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The specific input values from `[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m` that trigger this overflow[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The combination of parameters [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdimensions, chroma sampling, boolean flags[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat lead to incorrect buffer size calculations[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe investigation should focus on understanding why the buffer allocation or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary checks are insufficient for the particular combination of input parameters[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat triggers this overflow during the YUV to RGB conversion process.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the evaluation report and code snippets, I've identified two [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcritical issues in the `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` function in [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/libavif/src/[0m[95mreformat.c[0m[39m`:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Missing Boundary Checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m817[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The code accesses array elements [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith offsets `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, and `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` where `a` and `b` can be ±[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout checking if these indices are within bounds. This directly causes the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdynamic-stack-buffer-overflow.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Inappropriate Stack Allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m665[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m666[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Large Variable Length Arrays[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mVLAs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are allocated on the stack, which is dangerous for large images and can [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39measily cause stack overflow.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Add Missing Boundary Checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPrimary Fix for Immediate Issue[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: Before line [0m[1;36m810[0m[39m in `[0m[35m/src/libavif/src/[0m[95mreformat.c[0m[39m`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Add boundary checking logic similar to lines [0m[1;36m777[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[39m to protect the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray accesses at lines [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m817[0m[39m.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Steps**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. After line [0m[1;36m809[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere variables `a` and `b` are set[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add boundary checks:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `i + a < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, set `a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `i + a >= image->width`, set `a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `j + b < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, set `b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `j + b >= image->height`, set `b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This ensures that all accesses to `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, `vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, and `vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` remain within valid bounds.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification**: This follows the exact same pattern already established in the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase at lines [0m[1;36m777[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[39m, which successfully prevents out-of-bounds access for the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfirst set of spill operations. The pattern uses `adjCol` and `adjRow` variables [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith boundary checks, and we need to apply the same logic to variables `a` and `b`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix #[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Replace Stack Allocation with Heap Allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLong-term Robustness[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: Lines [0m[1;36m665[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m666[0m[39m and function exit points in [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/libavif/src/[0m[95mreformat.c[0m[39m`[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Replace stack-allocated VLAs with heap-allocated buffers.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Steps**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Replace the VLA declarations at lines [0m[1;36m665[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m666[0m[39m:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   float uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   float vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   With heap allocations using `[0m[1;35mavifAlloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   float * uspill_image = NULL;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   float * vspill_image = NULL;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. After line [0m[1;36m666[0m[39m, add allocation calls:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Calculate the required size: `size_t spillSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mimage->width * [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimage->height * [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfloat[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add overflow check for the multiplication[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Allocate: `uspill_image = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfloat*[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mavifAlloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mspillSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Check if allocation succeeded, if not return `AVIF_RESULT_OUT_OF_MEMORY`[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Allocate: `vspill_image = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfloat*[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mavifAlloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mspillSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Check if allocation succeeded, if not free `uspill_image` and return [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`AVIF_RESULT_OUT_OF_MEMORY`[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Change all 2D array accesses from `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mx[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39my[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` to `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mx * [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimage->height + y[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m1D indexing[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Before all return statements in the function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparticularly around line [0m[1;36m1126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madd cleanup:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mavifFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39muspill_image[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mavifFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvspill_image[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification**: [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The codebase already uses `[0m[1;35mavifAlloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mavifFree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for memory management [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mseen in avif.[0m[1;92mc:152[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Heap allocation prevents stack overflow for large images[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allows proper error handling if allocation fails[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with the existing memory management pattern in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avifFreeYUVToRGBLookUpTables` at line [0m[1;36m1126[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix #[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add Integer Overflow Protection[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: Before the allocation in Fix #[0m[1;36m2[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Add a check to prevent integer overflow when calculating buffer size.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Steps**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Before calculating `spillSize`, verify:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `image->width > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && image->height > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `image->width <= AVIF_DEFAULT_IMAGE_DIMENSION_LIMIT`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `image->height <= AVIF_DEFAULT_IMAGE_DIMENSION_LIMIT`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The multiplication won't overflow: `image->width <= SIZE_MAX [0m[35m/[0m[39m image->height [0m[35m/[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfloat[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. If any check fails, skip the spill upsampling code path or return an error.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification**: Prevents potential integer overflow in size calculations that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcould lead to undersized allocations and subsequent buffer overflows.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Why This Fix Strategy is Optimal[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses Root Cause**: Fix #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m directly addresses the buffer overflow by [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madding the missing boundary checks, following the existing pattern in the code.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: The boundary checking pattern already exists at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m777[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[39m and works correctly. We're simply applying the same logic to another [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocation where it was missing.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Improves Robustness**: Fix #[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m moves from dangerous stack allocation to safe [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap allocation, preventing stack overflow issues for large images.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Consistent with Codebase**: Uses `[0m[1;35mavifAlloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`[0m[1;35mavifFree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which are already [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused throughout the codebase for memory management.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Maintains Functionality**: The spill upsampling algorithm logic remains [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged; we're only changing how memory is allocated and adding safety checks.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: The function signature and API remain the same. The [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges are internal to the function implementation.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Proper Error Handling**: Adds appropriate error returns [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`AVIF_RESULT_OUT_OF_MEMORY`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m if heap allocation fails, which is better than stack [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Performance Impact**: Heap allocation is slightly slower than stack [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation, but this is negligible compared to the actual YUV-to-RGB conversion [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing time. The spill upsampling is already an expensive operation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mruns up to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m20[0m[39m iterations as seen at line [0m[1;36m681[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Fragmentation**: Large heap allocations might cause fragmentation, but [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis is acceptable given the safety benefits. The allocations are temporary and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed at function exit.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Index Calculation Changes**: Converting from 2D to 1D array indexing requires [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupdating all array accesses. This must be done carefully to avoid introducing new [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbugs. The pattern is straightforward: `arr[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` becomes `arr[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi * height + j[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Relation to Existing Code Patterns[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix follows established patterns in the codebase:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Boundary checking pattern from lines [0m[1;36m777[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory allocation pattern from avif.[0m[1;92mc:152[0m[39m using `[0m[1;35mavifAlloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory cleanup pattern from line [0m[1;36m1126[0m[39m using `[0m[1;35mavifFreeYUVToRGBLookUpTables[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Error return pattern returning `AVIF_RESULT_OUT_OF_MEMORY` on allocation failure[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
